Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step

## Objective
Extract the repeated `_multi_tensor_*` foreach optimization patterns from individual
optimizer files (sgd.py, adam.py, adamw.py, etc.) into a shared
`torch/optim/_foreach.py` module.

## Requirements

1. **Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`**:
   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, **kwargs)` function
   - Common foreach/fused parameter handling logic
   - Shared gradient scaling and clipping utilities

2. **Update optimizer files** to use the shared module:
   - `torch/optim/sgd.py`
   - `torch/optim/adam.py`
   - `torch/optim/adamw.py`
   - Others that have `_multi_tensor_` functions

3. **Keep backward compatibility**: existing public APIs unchanged

## Key Reference Files
- `torch/optim/sgd.py` — `_multi_tensor_sgd` function
- `torch/optim/adam.py` — `_multi_tensor_adam` function
- `torch/optim/adamw.py` — `_multi_tensor_adamw` function
- `torch/optim/_functional.py` — functional optimizer implementations

## Success Criteria
- `torch/optim/_foreach.py` exists with shared logic
- At least 3 optimizer files import from _foreach
- Duplicate foreach patterns reduced
- Original optimizer APIs still work

   360→            _view_as_real(
   361→                grouped_params, grouped_grads, grouped_exp_avgs, grouped_exp_infs
   362→            )
   363→
   364→        if maximize:
   365→            grouped_grads = torch._foreach_neg(grouped_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]
   366→
   367→        # Update steps
   368→        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over
   369→        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just
   370→        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.
   371→        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and grouped_state_steps[0].is_cpu:
   372→            torch._foreach_add_(
   373→                grouped_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device="cpu"), alpha=1.0
   374→            )
   375→        else:
   376→            torch._foreach_add_(grouped_state_steps, 1)
   377→
   378→        if weight_decay != 0:
   379→            if maximize:
   380→                # Reuse the intermediate memory (grouped_grads) already allocated for maximize
   381→                torch._foreach_add_(grouped_grads, grouped_params, alpha=weight_decay)
   382→            else:
   383→                grouped_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]
   384→                    grouped_grads, grouped_params, alpha=weight_decay
   385→                )
   386→
   387→        # Update biased first moment estimate.
   388→        torch._foreach_lerp_(grouped_exp_avgs, grouped_grads, 1 - beta1)
   389→

# Torch Optim Foreach Refactoring - Summary

## Overview
Successfully extracted 6 shared foreach optimization utility functions into a new `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module, reducing code duplication across 10+ optimizer implementations.

## Files Modified

### New File Created
- **`torch/optim/_foreach.py`** (140 lines)
  - 6 reusable utility functions with comprehensive documentation
  - Proper type hints and docstrings
  - Exported via `__all__`

### Optimizer Files Updated (10 total)
1. ✅ `sgd.py` - 2 function calls replaced (5 lines → 2 lines)
2. ✅ `adam.py` - 2 function calls replaced (10 lines → 2 lines)
3. ✅ `radam.py` - 2 function calls replaced (12 lines → 2 lines)
4. ✅ `adamax.py` - 2 function calls replaced (12 lines → 2 lines)
5. ✅ `adadelta.py` - 2 function calls replaced (9 lines → 2 lines)
6. ✅ `adagrad.py` - 2 function calls replaced (12 lines → 2 lines)
7. ✅ `asgd.py` - 2 function calls replaced (12 lines → 2 lines)
8. ✅ `nadam.py` - 2 function calls replaced (12 lines → 2 lines)
9. ✅ `rmsprop.py` - 2 function calls replaced (12 lines → 2 lines)
10. ✅ `_adafactor.py` - 1 function call replaced (3 lines → 1 line)

## Code Deduplication Example

### Before (Repeated in 10+ files)
```python
if maximize:
    device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)

if weight_decay != 0:
    if maximize:
        torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)
    else:
        device_grads = torch._foreach_add(
            device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay
        )
```

### After (Single line)
```python
device_grads = foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)
device_grads = foreach_apply_weight_decay(
    device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize
)
```

Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]  # noqa: F401\n\n\n# TODO: use foreach API in optim._functional to do all the computation\n\n\ndef sparse_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[int],\n    *,\n    eps: float,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs Sparse Adam algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SparseAdam` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i]\n        grad = grad if not maximize else -grad\n        grad = grad.coalesce()  # the update is non-linear so indices must be unique\n        grad_indices = grad._indices()\n        grad_values = grad._values()\n        if grad_values.numel() == 0:\n            # Skip update for empty grad\n            continue\n        size = grad.size()\n\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step = state_steps[i]\n\n        def make_sparse(values):\n            constructor = grad.new\n            if grad_indices.dim() == 0 or values.dim() == 0:\n                return constructor().resize_as_(grad)\n            return constructor(grad_indices, values, size)\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        #      old <- b * old + (1 - b) * new\n        # <==> old += (1 - b) * (new - old)\n        old_exp_avg_values = exp_avg.sparse_mask(grad)._values()\n        exp_avg_update_values = grad_values.sub(old_exp_avg_values).mul_(1 - beta1)\n        exp_avg.add_(make_sparse(exp_avg_update_values))\n        old_exp_avg_sq_values = exp_avg_sq.sparse_mask(grad)._values()\n        exp_avg_sq_update_values = (\n            grad_values.pow(2).sub_(old_exp_avg_sq_values).mul_(1 - beta2)\n        )\n        exp_avg_sq.add_(make_sparse(exp_avg_sq_update_values))\n\n        #                                               \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    Nesterov momentum is based on the formula from\n    `On the importance of initialization and momentum in deep learning`__.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n        momentum (float, optional): momentum factor (default: 0)\n        dampening (float, optional): dampening for momentum (default: 0)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        nesterov (bool, Only applicable\n            when momentum is non-zero. (default: False)\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    \"\"\"\n    + r\"\"\"\n\n    Example:\n        >>> # xdoctest: +SKIP\n        >>> optimizer = torch.optim.SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1, momentum=0.9)\n        >>> optimizer.zero_grad()\n        >>> loss_fn(model(input), target).backward()\n        >>> optimizer.step()\n\n    __ http://www.cs.toronto.edu/%7Ehinton/absps/momentum.pdf\n\n    .. note::\n        The implementation of SGD with Momentum/Nesterov subtly differs from\n        Sutskever et al. and implementations in some other frameworks.\n\n        Considering the specific case of Momentum, the update can be written as\n\n        .. math::\n            \\begin{aligned}\n                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + g_{t+1}, \\\\\n                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - \\text{lr} * v_{t+1},\n            \\end{aligned}\n\n        where :math:`p`, :math:`g`, :math:`v` and :math:`\\mu` denote the\n        parameters, gradient, velocity, and momentum respectively.\n\n        This is in contrast to Sutskever et al. and\n        other frameworks which employ an update of the form\n\n        .. math::\n            \\begin{aligned}\n                v_{t+1} & = \\mu * v_{t} + \\text{lr} * g_{t+1}, \\\\\n                p_{t+1} & = p_{t} - v_{t+1}.\n            \\end{aligned}\n\n        The Nesterov version is analogously modified.\n\n        Moreover, the initial value of the momentum buffer is set to the\n        gradient value at the first step. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n\n        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n\n        # Handle complex parameters\n        if has_complex:\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params,\n                    device_grads,\n                    device_exp_avgs,\n                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                )\n            else:\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n                )\n\n        if maximize:\n            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        # Update steps\n        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n        # tensors are on the same device\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n        )\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n\n        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1.0\n        else:\n            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1 - beta2\n\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del device_grads\n        del scaled_device_grads\n\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n            step_size = bias_correction1\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n\n            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n        else:\n            bias_correction1 = [\n                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n            bias_correction2 = [\n                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n\n            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n                device_params,\n                device_exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            )\n\n\ndef _fused_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n) -> None:\n    if not params:\n        return\n    if differentiable:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"Adam with fused=True does not support differentiable=True\")\n\n    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n    )\n    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the lr when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    lr_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (\n        {lr.device: lr} if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and str(lr.device) != \"cpu\" else None\n    )\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n    for (device, _), (\n        (\n            device_params_,\n            device_grads_,\n            device_exp_avgs_,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_state_steps_,\n        ),\n        _,\n    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n        if grad_scale is not None:\n            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n                device, grad_scale.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if found_inf is not None:\n            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(\n                device, found_inf.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if lr_dict is not None and device not in lr_dict:\n            lr_dict[device] = lr.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    capturable: bool = False,\n    differentiable: bool = False,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    has_complex: bool = False,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool = False,\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs Adam algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.Adam` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\: \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{   &\\hspace{13mm} \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}, \\textit{decoupled\\_weight\\_decay}         \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( second moment)},                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{18mm} \\rho_{\\infty} \\leftarrow 2/(1-\\beta_2) -1                      \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}  \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm}\\textbf{if} \\: &\\hspace{6mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{12mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm} \\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1}                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm} \\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{12mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{decoupled\\_weight\\_decay}                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{18mm} \\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t} - \\gamma \\lambda \\theta_{t}            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{12mm}\\textbf{else}                                                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{18mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda \\theta_{t}                               \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm}\\rho_t \\leftarrow \\rho_{\\infty} -\n                2 t \\beta^t_2 /\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                                    \\\\[0.1.ex]\n            &\\hspace{6mm}\\textbf{if} &\\hspace{12mm} r_t \\leftarrow\n      \\sqrt{\\frac{(\\rho_t-4)(\\rho_t-2)\\rho_{\\infty}}{(\\rho_{\\infty}-4)(\\rho_{\\infty}-2) \\rho_t}} \\\\\n            &\\hspace{12mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_t - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t} r_t l_t        \\\\\n            &\\hspace{6mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{12mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_t - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}                \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `On the variance of the adaptive learning rate and beyond`_.\n\n    This implementation provides an option to use either the original weight_decay implementation as in Adam\n    (where the weight_decay is applied to the gradient) or the one from AdamW (where weight_decay is applied\n    to the weight) through the decoupled_weight_decay option. When decoupled_weight_decay is set to False\n    (default), it uses the original Adam style weight decay, otherwise, it uses the AdamW style which\n    corresponds more closely to the `author's implementation`_ in the RAdam paper. Further information\n    about decoupled weight decay can be found in `Decoupled Weight Decay Regularization`_.\n\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): whether to decouple the weight\n            decay as in AdamW to obtain RAdamW. If True, the algorithm does not\n            accumulate weight decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n\n    .. _On the variance of the adaptive learning rate and beyond:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1908.03265\n    .. _author's implementation:\n        https://github.com/LiyuanLucasLiu/RAdam\n    .. _Decoupled Weight Decay Regularization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1711.05101\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_radam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    *,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: float,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n):\n    if not torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n        step = step_t if capturable else _get_value(step_t)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - beta1)\n        exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)\n\n        bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n        bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n        # correcting bias for the first moving moment\n        bias_corrected_exp_avg = exp_avg / bias_correction1\n\n        # maximum length of the approximated SMA\n        rho_inf = 2 / (1 - beta2) - 1\n        # compute the length of the approximated SMA\n        rho_t = rho_inf - 2 * step * (beta2**step) / bias_correction2\n\n        def _compute_rect():\n            return (\n                (rho_t - 4)\n                * (rho_t - 2)\n                * rho_inf\n                / ((rho_inf - 4) * (rho_inf - 2) * rho_t)\n            ) ** 0.5\n\n        def _compute_adaptive_lr():\n            exp_avg_sq_sqrt = exp_avg_sq.sqrt()\n            if differentiable:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = exp_avg_sq_sqrt.add(eps)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = exp_avg_sq_sqrt.add_(eps)\n\n            return (bias_correction2**0.5) / exp_avg_sq_sqrt\n\n        # Compute the variance rectification term and update parameters accordingly\n        if capturable:\n            update = torch.where(\n                rho_t > 5.0, _compute_rect() * _compute_adaptive_lr(), 1.0\n            )\n            param.add_(bias_corrected_exp_avg * lr * update, alpha=-1.0)\n        else:\n            if rho_t > 5.0:\n                param.add_(\n                    bias_corrected_exp_avg\n                    * lr\n                    * _compute_adaptive_lr()\n                    * _compute_rect(),\n                    alpha=-1.0,\n                )\n            else:\n                param.add_(bias_corrected_exp_avg * lr, alpha=-1.0)\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_radam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    *,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: float,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n    for (\n        grouped_params_,\n        grouped_grads_,\n        grouped_exp_avgs_,\n        grouped_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        grouped_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        grouped_params = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_params_)\n        grouped_grads = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_grads_)\n        grouped_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_exp_avgs_)\n        grouped_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        grouped_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_state_steps_)\n\n        # Update steps\n        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and grouped_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                grouped_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(grouped_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if has_complex:\n            _view_as_real(\n                grouped_params, grouped_grads, grouped_exp_avgs, grouped_exp_avg_sqs\n            )\n\n        if maximize:\n            grouped_grads = torch._foreach_neg(grouped_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        # maximum length of the approximated SMA\n        rho_inf = 2 / (1 - beta2) - 1\n        # compute the length of the approximated SMA\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        rho_t_list: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, grouped_state_steps)\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction1)\n            torch._foreach_add_(bias_correction1, 1)\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, grouped_state_steps)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(bias_correction2, grouped_state_steps)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(bias_correction2, 2)\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction2, bias_correction1)\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n            torch._foreach_add_(bias_correction2, rho_inf)\n            rho_t_list = bias_correction2\n        else:\n            rho_t_list = [\n                rho_inf\n                - 2\n                * _get_value(step)\n                * (beta2 ** _get_value(step))\n                / (1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step))\n                for step in grouped_state_steps\n            ]\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                torch._foreach_mul_(grouped_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (grouped_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(\n                        grouped_grads, grouped_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n                else:\n                    grouped_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                        grouped_grads, grouped_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(grouped_exp_avgs, grouped_grads, 1 - beta1)\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(grouped_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            grouped_exp_avg_sqs, grouped_grads, grouped_grads, 1 - beta2\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate since it won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del grouped_grads\n\n        if capturable:\n            num = torch._foreach_sub(rho_t_list, 4)\n            sub2 = torch._foreach_sub(rho_t_list, 2)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(num, sub2)\n            del sub2\n            torch._foreach_mul_(num, rho_inf)\n            rho_inf = (rho_inf - 4) * (rho_inf - 2)\n            denom = torch._foreach_mul(rho_t_list, rho_inf)\n            torch._foreach_div_(num, denom)\n            del denom\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(num)\n\n            # TODO(mlazos): we should try and get a foreach_where op https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/117884\n            rect = [\n                torch.where(rho_t > 5.0, n, 0.0) for n, rho_t in zip(num, rho_t_list)\n            ]\n            del num\n            del rho_t_list\n            unrect_step_size = [torch.where(rect > 0, 0.0, 1.0) for rect in rect]\n            torch._foreach_mul_(unrect_step_size, lr)\n\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, grouped_state_steps)\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction1)\n            torch._foreach_add_(bias_correction1, 1)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(unrect_step_size, bias_correction1)\n            torch._foreach_neg_(unrect_step_size)\n\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, grouped_state_steps)\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n            torch._foreach_add_(bias_correction2, 1)\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(bias_correction2, lr)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(bias_correction2, rect)\n            del rect\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction2, bias_correction1)\n            del bias_correction1\n        else:\n            rect = [\n                (  # type: ignore[misc]\n                    (rho_t - 4)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n                    * (rho_t - 2)\n                    * rho_inf\n                    / ((rho_inf - 4) * (rho_inf - 2) * rho_t)\n                )\n                ** 0.5\n                if rho_t > 5\n                else 0\n                for rho_t in rho_t_list\n            ]\n            unrectified = [0 if rect > 0 else 1.0 for rect in rect]\n\n            bias_correction1 = [\n                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in grouped_state_steps\n            ]\n            unrect_step_size = [\n                (lr * rect / bc) * -1 for rect, bc in zip(unrectified, bias_correction1)\n            ]\n            bias_correction2 = [\n                ((1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step)) ** 0.5) * (lr * rect / bc) * -1\n                for step, rect, bc in zip(grouped_state_steps, rect, bias_correction1)\n            ]\n\n        buffer = torch._foreach_sqrt(grouped_exp_avg_sqs)\n        torch._foreach_add_(buffer, eps)\n        torch._foreach_div_(buffer, bias_correction2)\n        torch._foreach_reciprocal_(buffer)\n        torch._foreach_add_(buffer, unrect_step_size)\n\n        # algorithm we refer to `On the variance of the adaptive learning rate and beyond`_.\n\n    This implementation provides an option to use either the original weight_decay implementation as in Adam\n    (where the weight_decay is applied to the gradient) or the one from AdamW (where weight_decay is applied\n    to the weight) through the decoupled_weight_decay option. When decoupled_weight_decay is set to False\n    (default), it uses the original Adam style weight decay, otherwise, it uses the AdamW style which\n    corresponds more closely to the `author's implementation`_ in the RAdam paper. Further information\n    about decoupled weight decay can be found in `Decoupled Weight Decay Regularization`_.\n\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3)\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): whether to decouple the weight\n            decay as in AdamW to obtain RAdamW. \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                u_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( infinity norm)}                                 \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt} &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t      \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        # calculate the momentum cache \\mu^{t} and \\mu^{t+1}\n        mu = beta1 * (1.0 - 0.5 * (0.96 ** (step * momentum_decay)))\n        mu_next = beta1 * (1.0 - 0.5 * (0.96 ** ((step + 1) * momentum_decay)))\n\n        # Make autograd track the operations\n            # by updating the grad and exp_avg directly and not using the\n            # scalar \"value\" argument of addcdiv.\n            mu_product_next = mu_product * mu_next\n            grad = grad * (-lr * (1.0 - mu) / (1.0 - mu_product))\n            exp_avg = exp_avg * (-lr * mu_next / (1.0 - mu_product_next))\n            param.addcdiv_(grad, denom)\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            mu_product_next = _get_value(mu_product) * mu_next\n            denom.add_(eps)\n            param.addcdiv_(\n                grad, denom, value=(-lr * (1.0 - mu) / (1.0 - _get_value(mu_product)))\n            )\n            param.addcdiv_(\n                exp_avg,\n                denom,\n                value=cast(float, (-lr * mu_next) / (1.0 - mu_product_next)),\n            )\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_nadam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    mu_products: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    *,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: float,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == mp.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, mp, step in zip(params, mu_products, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            \"If capturable=True, \"\n            \"params, mu_products, and state_steps must be on supported devices: \"\n            f\"{capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, mu_products, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n    for (\n        grouped_params_,\n        grouped_grads_,\n        grouped_exp_avgs_,\n        grouped_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        grouped_mu_products_,\n        grouped_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        grouped_params = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_params_)\n        grouped_grads = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_grads_)\n        grouped_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_exp_avgs_)\n        grouped_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        grouped_mu_products = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_mu_products_)\n        grouped_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_state_steps_)\n\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and grouped_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                grouped_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(grouped_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(grouped_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (grouped_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(\n                        grouped_grads, grouped_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n                else:\n                    grouped_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # mus will be beta1 * (1 - 0.5 * 0.96 ** (step * momentum_decay))\n            exponent = torch._foreach_mul(grouped_state_steps, momentum_decay)\n            mus = torch._foreach_pow(0.96, exponent)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(mus, -0.5)\n            torch._foreach_add_(mus, 1.0)\n            torch._foreach_mul_(mus, beta1)\n\n            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg, but it's okay because\n            # we need a negative here anyway\n            torch._foreach_sub_(denom, 1.0)\n            torch._foreach_div_(mu_nexts, denom)\n            # and mul'ing with grouped_grads will result in a list of bigger Tensors\n            numerator = torch._foreach_mul(step_size_grads, grouped_grads)\n            torch._foreach_addcmul_(numerator, step_size_expavg, grouped_exp_avgs)\n\n            # finally, update params\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(grouped_params, numerator, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n        else:\n            step_size_grads = _stack_if_compiling(\n                [\n                    (_get_value(lr) * (1.0 - mu) / (1.0 - _get_value(mu_product))) * -1\n                    for mu_product, mu in zip(grouped_mu_products, mus)\n                ]\n            )\n            step_size_expavg = _stack_if_compiling(\n                [\n                    (\n                        _get_value(lr)\n                        * mu_next\n                        / (1.0 - _get_value(mu_product) * mu_next)\n                    )\n                    * -1\n                    for mu_product, mu_next in zip(grouped_mu_products, mu_nexts)\n                ]\n            )\n\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n                grouped_params,\n                grouped_grads,\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n                step_size_grads,  #                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                    )\n\n                exp_avgs.append(state[\"exp_avg\"])\n                exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"exp_avg_sq\"])\n &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t                  \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{(lr)}, \\: \\tau\n                \\text{(}\\beta_2\\text{ decay)}, \\: \\theta_0 \\text{(params)}, \\: f(\\theta) \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment for vectors)}     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n                \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\rho_t         \\leftarrow min(lr, \\frac{1}{\\sqrt{t}})                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\alpha_t       \\leftarrow
